 Two days after the demonetisation on November 8 last year, new notes of Rs 2,000 were issued in the market in large quantities
 lekin 500 rupee ke note ko aane main lanbaa vakt lag gaya, jiske kaaran lakhon logon ko kai dinon tak pareshaani jhelni padi
 Have you ever wondered why this happened? Here are some information provided by a top official related to this issue
 - jab notebandi kii ghoshnaa kii gai thi, tababhartiya rigerv bank(arabiai) ke paas 2,000 rupee ke nae noton kaa 4
 There was a stock of 95 lakh crores, but he did not have a single note of the new 500 rupees
 is note ke bare main baad main sochaa gaya
 There are four printing presses in the country to print notes
 inamen arabiai ke do press hai, jo mysore (karnataka) or salboni (pashchim bengal) main hai
 Apart from this, Securities Printing and Currency Manufacturing Corporation of India Ltd
 (espmasiiel) ke do printing press hai, jo nasik (maharashtra) or devas (madhya pradesh) main hai
 SPMCIL is a wholly owned government company, which was established in 2006 for printing of notes, minting of coins and printing of non-judicial stamps
 - espmasiiel hameshaa arabiai dwaara die gaye order ke mutabiknoton kii chapaikarti he
 But this time SPMCIL started printing the notes without an official RBI order
 500 rupee ke note kii dizin notebandi se pehle keval arabiai ke mysore press ke paas tha
 - It started printing in the second week of November in Nashik Press in the fourth week of November without official RBI order in Dewas Press of SPMCIL
 haalanki isaki chapai arabiai ke press main pehle se kii ja rahi thi, lekin vah notebandi ke kaaran badi maang ko puraa nahin kar paa rahaa tha
 - It usually takes 40 days to print a note, including the time taken to purchase paper according to the new design
 notebandi ke kaaran isamen teji laane ke liye is avadhi ko ghataakar 22 din kar diya gaya
 The paper and ink used to print the note are purchased from other countries, which takes 30 days to arrive
 lekin notebandi ke baad hui pareshaani ko dekhte hue ise vimaan se do din main laayaa ja rahaa tha
 It takes 10–11 days from RBI to take notes in its remote chest, which is 1–1 by helicopter and ship
 5 din main pahunchaaya gaya
 - The paper which is inserted in the printing press to print the note, is equipped with high sensory security thread and after 16 days it is printed out
 - lekin pehali baar desh main bane hue kaagaj kaa istemaal 500 rupee ke note chhapane main kiya gaya
 This paper was developed at paper mills in Hoshangabad and Mysore
 lekin unki kshamta 12,000 metric ton salanaa he, jo paryaapt nahin he or abhi bhi iske aayaat kii jarurat padati he
 spmcil's Nashik and Dewas Press used ink made by them to print 500 rupee notes, whereas the ink that RBI uses in its press comes from other countries
 - nasik or devas press kii note chhapane kii sanyukt kshamta 7
 2 billion notes annually
 jabaki arabiai ke mysore or salboni press kii sanyukt kshamta 16 arab note salanaa chhapane kii he
 After demonetisation, 200 people were sent by the Ministry of Defense to work in these printing presses and the help of 100 retired employees of these presses was also taken
 - empmasiiel ne 30 disambar tak 500 rupee ke 90 karod note chhapane kaa lakshya rakhaa he
 Since January, it has been printing 30 crore notes every month
 - arabiai or espmasiiel main 500 rupee kaa note 60 or 40 ke anupaat main chhapata he, jabaki 2000 rupee kaa note sirf arabiai ke preson main hi chapa jaataa he
 - There are reports that the printing of 2000 rupee notes has been reduced and the government has ordered to print 500 rupee notes in its place
 - yahi kaaran he ki notebandi ke baad disambar ke ant tak hi bazaar main 500 rupee ke note aane ke baad logon ko thodi raahat mili thi

 Eid Ul Fitr 2019 Date and Moon News: When it comes to Eid, the first mention comes of Eid ka Chand
 id kaa chand ramajaan (ramadan 2019) ke 30wein roze ke baad hi dikhataa he
 Eid is celebrated by seeing this moon
 hijri calendar (islamic Calendar 2019), joki islamic calendar he, ke anusaar id saal main do baar aati he
 One is eid-eid-ul-fitr (2019 Eid Ul Fitr) and the other is called eid-ul-juha
 id-ul-fitar ko mahaj id bhi kaha jaataa he
 Apart from this, it is also called Meethi Eid 2019
 jabaki id-ul-juha ko bakreed (bakra Eid 2019) ke naam se bhi janaa jaataa he
 Now come to the question on which day Eid is celebrated (eid Kab Hai 2019)
 to jis din id kaa chand najar aata he id bhi usee din manaai jaati he
 This is the reason that many times Eid can be celebrated on different days in the same country
 jahaan chand pehle dekha jaataa he vahaan id pehle man jaati he
 
 
 It is clear from this that there is some special relationship between Eid and Chand
 aaie aaj aapako bataate hai ki id or chand ke bich he kya special conection

 Shawwal ul-muqaram, the tenth month of Hijri calendar (hijri Samvat)
 ab samajhane vaali baat yah bhi he ki hijri calendar kii shuruyaat islam kii ek prasiddh aitihaasik ghatana se maani jaati he
 The incident is that of Hazrat Muhammad moving from Mecca City to Medina, when Hazrat Muhammad left Mecca and traveled to Medina
 hijri samvath jis hijri calendar kaa hissaa he vah chand par aadhaarit calendar he
 Every month in this calendar is considered to start by seeing the new moon
 thik isi tarj par shavwaal maheenaa bhi ‘nayaa chand' dekh kar hi shuru hota he
 And according to Hijri calendar, the month after Ramadan is Shawwal
 aise main jab tak shavwaal kaa pehla chand najar nahin aata ramajaan ke maheene ko puraa nahin mana jaataa
 There are many benefits of drinking warm water before bedtime, try it out shavwaal kaa chand najar na aane par mana jaataa he ki ramajaan kaa maheenaa mukammal hone main kami he
 For this reason, Eid is celebrated the next day or whenever the moon is seen
 or khabaron ke liye clic karen The Hijri calendar which is part of the Hijri calendar is a moon-based calendar
 is calendar main har maheenaa nayaa chand dekhakar hi shuru mana jaataa he
 On the same lines, the month of Shawwal also begins by seeing the 'new moon'
 or hijri calendar ke mutabik ramajaan ke baad aane vaala maheenaa hota he shavwaal
 In such a situation, the month of Ramadan is not considered complete until the first moon of Shawwal is seen
